Change_Primary_pommeranian = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = majority_pommeranian_primary
		}
		remove_province_modifier = majority_pommeranian_primary
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = majority_pommeranian_accepted
			desc = majority_pommeranian_accepted_desc
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = majority_pommeranian_primary
		}
		remove_province_modifier = majority_pommeranian_primary
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = majority_pommeranian_accepted
			desc = majority_pommeranian_accepted_desc
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = majority_pommeranian_primary
		}
		remove_province_modifier = majority_pommeranian_primary
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = majority_pommeranian_accepted
			desc = majority_pommeranian_accepted_desc
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
